6017 = {
	name = "Amato, Luigi"
	country = ITA add_trait = ITA_tag
	type = land
	skill = 1 # WW1 veteran, mediocre commander, yet valorous-he escaped on foot for hundreds of km in Lybian desert, personally fighting several British patrols
	max_skill = 7
	loyalty = 1.00
	picture = L6017
	add_trait = fortress_buster # commander of 10o Rgt. Artiglieria in 1935-36. In 1937-38 he led the artillery units of Corpo Truppe Volontarie in Spain
 	add_trait = logistics_wizard # Chief of Staff, 4a Armata 1939.08.25–1940.06.XX, then 1940.06.XX–1940.12.XX Chief of Staff, 7th Army
	add_trait = National_medal # 1929.05.29, 3rd of the 5 ranks of Albanian Order of Skanderbeg
	add_trait = Order_of_the_Crown_of_Italy # actually in 1941.08.24, 4th rank out of 5, added for flavour
	add_trait = Order_of_Military_Medal # actually in 1942.12.24, 1st rank out of 5 added for flavour
	add_trait = For_Valor_Silver_Medal # twice, once in WW1 once in Spain, plus 2 bronze and one gold medals
	add_trait = Corpo_Truppe_Volontarie # should get in 1937, only way to give it to him
	history = {
		1940.1.1 = { rank = 1 } # actually Major-General 1942.01.01, but he commanded 64a Div. Fanteria 'Catanzaro' in 1940 in Lybia-later, he led 32a Div. Fanteria 'Marche' in Yugoslavia in 1941-43 before being executed by Germans
		1944.1.1 = { rank = 0 }
	}
}
